## Summary

### Conversion Functions Between Versions

The Ingress API conversion goes through an internal representation. Three sets of conversion files handle this:

1. **`pkg/apis/networking/v1beta1/conversion.go`** - Manual conversion functions for `networking.k8s.io/v1beta1` ↔ internal (handles `IngressBackend` service name/port mapping, `IngressSpec` default backend)
2. **`pkg/apis/networking/v1beta1/zz_generated.conversion.go`** - Generated conversions for all Ingress types
3. **`pkg/apis/extensions/v1beta1/conversion.go`** - Same manual conversions for the deprecated `extensions/v1beta1` group
4. **`pkg/apis/extensions/v1beta1/zz_generated.conversion.go`** - Generated conversions for extensions v1beta1
5. **`pkg/apis/networking/v1/zz_generated.conversion.go`** - Generated conversions for `networking.k8s.io/v1` ↔ internal

### Validation Changes (pathType became required)

- **`pkg/apis/networking/validation/validation.go`** - `validateHTTPIngressPath` returns `field.Required` error if `pathType == nil`; `IngressValidationOptions` struct controls beta-to-GA transitions
- **`pkg/apis/networking/v1beta1/defaults.go`** - `SetDefaults_HTTPIngressPath` defaults pathType to `ImplementationSpecific` for v1beta1 compatibility
- **`pkg/apis/extensions/v1beta1/defaults.go`** - Same defaulting for extensions/v1beta1

### Storage Version Migration Logic

- **`pkg/kubeapiserver/default_storage_factory_builder.go`** - `AddCohabitatingResources` makes `networking.k8s.io/ingresses` and `extensions/ingresses` share the same etcd storage path (`/registry/ingress/`)
- **`pkg/controlplane/storageversionhashdata/data.go`** - Records `networking.k8s.io/v1` as the storage version

Without sorting, in an HA cluster, one\n        // apiserver may dedup and update StorageVersion for extensions.ingresses,\n        // while another apiserver may dedup and update StorageVersion for\n        // networking.k8s.io.ingresses. The StorageVersion manager\n// only needs to update one StorageVersion for the equivalent Groups.\nfunc dedupResourceInfos(infos []ResourceInfo) []ResourceInfo {\n        var ret []ResourceInfo\n        seen := make(map[schema.GroupResource]struct{})\n        for _, info := range infos {\n                gr := info.GroupResource\n                if _, ok := seen[gr]; ok {\n                        continue\n                }\n                gvrs := info.EquivalentResourceMapper.EquivalentResourcesFor(gr.WithVersion(\"\"), \"\")\n                for _, gvr := range gvrs {\n                        seen[gvr.GroupResource()] = struct{}{}\n                }\n                ret = append(ret, info)\n        }\n        return ret\n}\n\nfunc sortResourceInfosByGroupResource(infos []ResourceInfo) {\n        sort.Sort(byGroupResource(infos))\n}\n\ntype byGroupResource []ResourceInfo\n\nfunc (s byGroupResource) Len() int { return len(s) }\n\nfunc (s byGroupResource) Less(i, j int) bool {\n        if s[i].GroupResource.Group == s[j].GroupResource.Group {"
